msg:Pan Pacific is rated as outstanding and a 5* experience but we‚Äôve stayed 5* in Beijing many times and this hotel is definitely not anywhere near those stays, however, there are some aspects which do reflect 5* service so I‚Äôll begin my review with the positives: 

1. 5* service in the Western restaurant, particularly from Fisher, Tong and the main chef. The dinner buffet was fantastic and definitely worth it. We didn‚Äôt visit the other restaurants so cannot comment on the service there. 

2. A lot of the staff speak English which is helpful as our Mandarin is limited. 

3. Gym is great and well equipped. 

4. The rooftop bar is lovely especially in the evening. Only downside is that is closes at 11pm. 

5. The location of the hotel is good as it is right next door to Joy City shopping mall which also has a number of restaurants.  

6. The ayis and door staff are very friendly and welcoming and do a great job. 

7. The bed is very comfortable and the bathtub is huge, although the water is lukewarm. 

Reasons this hotel is not a 5* establishment in our eyes: 

1. Upon arrival to the hotel, the front desk reception was very cold and unwelcoming. One person in particular, who I shall not name continued with this attitude throughout our 3 day stay and was unwilling to assist with several of the issues mentioned below as when I approached the desk, he walked away, leaving his colleague who spoke less English than he, struggled to understand my complaints. 

2. Upon check-in, a staff member took 1000¬• as a deposit, despite us already paying for our stay online. This staff member didn‚Äôt bother explaining what the deposit was for he just simply said it was needed. I later found out, after enquiring myself, that it‚Äôs for additional charges such as in house dining. If this is the case and the deposit isn‚Äôt for potential damage caused to the room, then it should be properly explained and made optional. 

3. Before coming to the hotel I had called to ask if the pool, jacuzzi and steam room would be open and the front desk confirmed that they were. There is no steam room. The jacuzzi is weirdly in the changing rooms and was closed due to covid yet the pool was open and completely packed. We visited the pool at 9pm at night and there were tons of children, screaming and taking up most of the space with their floats. If this hotel is 5* there should be swimming hours in place for adults and children. We unfortunately didn‚Äôt use the pool at all during our stay because of this. 

4. Wifi is terrible, we gave up in the end. 

5. No room service which you‚Äôd expect in a 5* hotel. 

6. It was way too hot in the room and air con didn‚Äôt work well despite being on the lowest setting, however, the front desk staff were very helpful when I called down and provided a fan upon request, without it we wouldn‚Äôt have managed the stay. 

7. There are more minor complaints but still relevant when comparing where to stay in Beijing: 

- TV in the room is very small. 
- Design of the hotel is old fashioned and maybe more suited to local tastes. 
- Toiletries are stingy for a 5* hotel, tiniest ones I‚Äôve seen. 
- The coffee advertised in the room isn‚Äôt the ones you get, instead you get much cheaper ones and the taste is poor. 
- Old and very used towels, dressing gowns, carpets, and bedsheets. Our bedsheets actually had tea or coffee stains on them from previous usage. 
- Some of the furniture in the room is old and broken in addition to some of the lights/electrics being broken too. 

In summary, I wouldn‚Äôt ever stay here again. When I raised the issues above with the front desk they had nothing to offer other than sending someone to ‚Äòfix it‚Äô although I‚Äôm not sure what they were hoping to fix as that wasn‚Äôt made clear. 

Front desk staff definitely need additional training on welcoming guests and providing 5* customer service.

msg:As a senior hotel guest, I have four years of experience in family travel hotel accommodation. I rarely spend time commenting. This hotel is so bad that I have to feel a sense of mission and post it to help everyone avoid thunder.

Service: Six people can't understand one thing. The service level can also be seen below.

Price: The actual facilities are inconsistent with the pictures and have nothing to do with each other. This room type is actually a castrated version of "double room + suite", room 1515 + room 1511. The price of a four-person suite that opens the connecting door is more expensive than the most expensive "double room" + "suite" booked separately. What's so expensive? It's expensive for parent-child equipment, such as slide tents, children's mattresses and toiletries. However, surprisingly, it was not provided, and it looked the same as adults. So why should I spend more than the sum of two rooms to book a castrated room?
When we checked in, the manager asked us why we stayed for three nights and only booked one night. He said that it is difficult to book during holidays now, and we can confirm whether to renew as soon as possible. I said, I want to take the child's feelings as the standard, and try it for one night first, but why are there no parent-child facilities when we come in? He was stunned. After one round of communication, the explanation was that the last round of guests did not need it, so they left.
Excuse me? Sir? Do you really think this place is rare? Doesn't the cloth room need to be restored to a parent-child room? Didn't the front desk see the child and think of the reason why we booked a family room?
If you are not a parent-child room, why is the price higher? Finally, after two days of communication, the parent-child equipment was gradually completed and assembled on site.

Facilities: Room 1515 had abnormal power supply for two consecutive days, the phone was out of power, the TV was out of power, and any socket was out of power. The engineer had to repair the electrical box to restore it. Other facilities were old and of poor quality.

Room service: Chinese, Western, and Japanese food are on the same menu, but they are provided by two restaurants respectively. Ordering meals cannot be solved by one phone call. You have to call the two restaurants separately and order them separately, and you have to call the main desk every time.

Alas... I brought my children here to receive patriotic education, but the service quality under the imperial city is really worrying.

This hotel is really not worth the price. Apart from the good location of the hotel, I really can't find any other advantages.

1. Service
Basically no services.
The receptionist at the hotel entrance just stood next to the heater. Even when he saw the passengers pulling their suitcases in and out, they refused to help with their luggage or open the door. They didn't even say hello. It's chilling to see them looking so lazy every time you walk through the door.
What is the purpose of the existence of the staff in your hotel?

When I arrived at the hotel, there was a passenger in front of me who was checking in first. In addition to the staff who were handling business, there were two staff members. They clearly saw me waiting in line, but they kept chatting unceremoniously and kept me waiting. Later, before it was my turn, there was another passenger coming behind me to check in. The waiter who had been chatting with me just now greeted me and started handling business for me.
I wonder if your eyes don't work well? Didn't you see me just now? I've been waiting in line.
The key is that after waiting for a long time, they only gave me the room card without any apology, without any introduction about the breakfast time and location, elevator location, wifi password and other hotel facilities. Is this the service of a so-called five-star hotel?

Also, as others have said in negative reviews, even if you meet the staff in the elevator corridor, they basically won't say hello to you, it's almost like they can't see you.

2. Hygiene
There is only one sentence, "extremely bad"
There was a toothbrush case in the toiletry box that had been opened by the previous passenger, and there were stains and dust on the toiletry box. It looked like it hadn't been cleaned every time.
Whether in the room or in the corridor, you can easily see long hair, dust, etc., and the overall impression is that it is unhygienic. At that time, I bit the bullet and allowed myself to be tolerant and think that it might be an accident. Let‚Äôs see again.
As a result, after staying there for three days, it was still not cleaned.
Also, I stayed for three days and the sheets and pillowcases were not changed once. People who like to sleep on a clean hotel bed should take note.
The most disgusting thing is that when the staff came back to the room after cleaning the room the next day, they found brown stains on the flush button of the toilet, but I didn't notice it on the first day. I thought it was something rusty or something, but my God, when I lightly rubbed it with my finger, it turned out to be brown stolen goods.
I hesitated to call the staff to complain, but I originally wanted to travel and relax during the Spring Festival holiday, and I thought that even if I complained, such a bad hotel would not give a satisfactory answer. At most, it would be a quarrel and a waste of time, so I endured it for a while.

3. Breakfast
As others have said in negative reviews, the breakfast content is lacking and cannot be expected from a five-star hotel.
The breakfast location is behind the front desk on the first floor. You need to wear a coat to have breakfast on a cold day in Beijing. Can't expect a comfortable breakfast time.

4. wifi
slow Internet speed.
